<Rate>4< /Rate>< text>
Sushiman is definitely a great place for great portions, when you order sushi it comes with salad,gyozas and edamame.  Their food is on the average side nothing really stands out as excellent but none of it is bad.  Their sushi rolls are a good size and good quality,They have free refills on sodas but they only have one size which is fine.  Everytime I've eaten here it has been a good experience, friendly staff and your food gets to you pretty quickly after ordering. The location is a bit on the small size so during busy times it can get cramped. I have not tried their sashimi so I cant speak on the quality of that.  Overall I highly recommend this place to anyone who wants sushi and wants to get filled up for a good price.< /text>

< review>
If you're a seafood lover, the fish is not the HIGHEST quality of fish. But I recommend their Crunch rolls and all other basic rolls that aren't fishy (california, philly, spam) because they are very good. Fresh avocado, fresh rice, melts in your mouth. And their miso soup is great. They have specials, and the price is already low. ($3 or so for a hand roll which is 4 rolls, $8 or so for a plate that's more than double of that.<//review>
